benchmark-kafka
===============

### Running Benchmark

1. Start containers

   ```sh
   ./download.sh
   docker-compose up
   ```

2. Verify setup

   ```sh
   curl http://localhost:9639/metrics # scriptable-jmx-exporter
   curl http://localhost:9404/metrics # jmx_exporter
   ```

3. Apply load

   ```sh
   CONTAINER_IP=$(docker inspect benchmark-kafka_kafka_1 -f '{{ with (index .NetworkSettings.Networks "benchmark-kafka_default") }}{{ .IPAddress }}{{ end }}')
   for i in {0..9}; do wrk -d 10 -t `nproc` -c `nproc` "http://$CONTAINER_IP:9639/metrics"; done
   for i in {0..9}; do wrk -d 10 -t `nproc` -c `nproc` "http://$CONTAINER_IP:9404/metrics"; done
   ```

##### Differences in metric name and labels between the exporters

In this benchmark setup, the response of the two exporters are not completely identical. I tried to reduce the differences, but I leave them as they are where they should be. Here are the kafka-related differences:

```console
$ python diff_metrics.py "http://localhost:9404/metrics" "http://localhost:9639/metrics" "kafka.*"

# scriptable-jmx-exporter always unquotes key property values
- kafka_log_logcleanermanager_uncleanable_bytes{logDirectory="\"/bitnami/kafka/data\"",}
+ kafka_log_logcleanermanager_uncleanable_bytes{logDirectory="/bitnami/kafka/data",}

# scriptable-jmx-exporter always unquotes key property values
- kafka_log_logcleanermanager_uncleanable_partitions_count{logDirectory="\"/bitnami/kafka/data\"",}
+ kafka_log_logcleanermanager_uncleanable_partitions_count{logDirectory="/bitnami/kafka/data",}

# scriptable-jmx-exporter always unquotes key property values
- kafka_log_logmanager_logdirectoryoffline{logDirectory="\"/bitnami/kafka/data\"",}
+ kafka_log_logmanager_logdirectoryoffline{logDirectory="/bitnami/kafka/data",}

# kafka.network:type=Acceptor,listener=PLAINTEXT,name=AcceptorBlockedPercent is JmxReporter$Meter and thus should be a counter with `total` suffix for consistency
- kafka_network_acceptor_acceptorblockedpercent_count{listener="PLAINTEXT",}
+ kafka_network_acceptor_acceptorblockedpercent_total{listener="PLAINTEXT",}

# label orders can change
- kafka_network_requestmetrics_errors_total{request="UpdateMetadata",error="NONE",}
+ kafka_network_requestmetrics_errors_total{error="NONE",request="UpdateMetadata",}

# kafka.server:type=KafkaRequestHandlerPool,name=RequestHandlerAvgIdlePercent is JmxReporter$Meter and thus should be a counter with `total` suffix for consistency
- kafka_server_kafkarequesthandlerpool_requesthandleravgidlepercent_count
+ kafka_server_kafkarequesthandlerpool_requesthandleravgidlepercent_total

# kafka.utils:type=Throttler,name=cleaner-io is JmxReporter$Meter and thus should be a counter with `total` suffix for consistency
- kafka_utils_throttler_cleaner_io_count
+ kafka_utils_throttler_cleaner_io_total
```

I only compared the names and labels of kafka metrics. Their HELP texts are different.
Also, JMX metrics (MBeans in `java.*` domain) exposed by scriptable-jmx-exporter are vastly different to that of jmx_exporter's.
